Comment: unobtanium120 said "Borrowed this photo from @battlefrogseries of the top 2 male elite racers crossing the #Ropetraverse (#Tyroleantraverse). At approx 100 ft, this was the longest of these types of obstacles I've faced yet.  The real challenge came from the composition of the ropes.  Unlike #SpartanRace's spectra ropes, these ropes were not slippery at all.  The "under-rope" technique was physically exhausting due to the amount of friction caused by the trailing feet and legs, while the "over-rope" technique was extremely painful as that same friction created awful rope burns. 
After 2 failed attempts I was physically drained, mentally dejected, and in terrible pain.  I swam for the opposite shore to admit defeat and run on.  When I was close enough to stand, I looked up and saw the volunteer waiting to collect my Elite wristband.  At that moment it hit me; why do we do this?  Why do we love #OCR? Why do we push our bodies to the limit every weekend?  It's to know what we're really made of!  To know know when life gets tough, if we have what it takes inside to fight on, to persevere at all costs.  If it wasn't for this sport, when would I really ever get the chance to give everything I've  got.  I immediately turned around and swam back across to rejoin the other athletes battling the ropes for a third attempt.

At that point, Ryan Atkins was already sipping a latte and reading the Miami Herald back in the festival area. The top 10 males had crossed the finish line long ago.  There was no check with my name on it and no trophy.  That orange wristband and an unshakeable sense of pride in accomplishment were all that was left to take home.  I wasn't about to let that go. 
On my third attempt, I painfully crawled along the top of the rope for about 50 ft before slipping under. That's when my will took over.  I WAS NOT GOING BACK!  Hand over hand, foot over foot, I muscled across and finally made it.  #nevergiveup  Sometimes timing and ranking just don't matter.  I will be wearing that wristband for at least a week. 👊 🐸 💪"

Comment: unobtanium120 said "Borrowed this photo from @battlefrogseries of the top 2 male elite racers crossing the #Ropetraverse (#Tyroleantraverse). At approx 100 ft, this was the longest of these types of obstacles I've faced yet.  The real challenge came from the composition of the ropes.  Unlike #SpartanRace's spectra ropes, these ropes were not slippery at all.  The "under-rope" technique was physically exhausting due to the amount of friction caused by the trailing feet and legs, while the "over-rope" technique was extremely painful as that same friction created awful rope burns. 
After 2 failed attempts I was physically drained, mentally dejected, and in terrible pain.  I swam for the opposite shore to admit defeat and run on.  When I was close enough to stand, I looked up and saw the volunteer waiting to collect my Elite wristband.  At that moment it hit me; why do we do this?  Why do we love #OCR? Why do we push our bodies to the limit every weekend?  It's to know what we're really made of!  To know know when life gets tough, if we have what it takes inside to fight on, to persevere at all costs.  If it wasn't for this sport, when would I really ever get the chance to give everything I've  got.  I immediately turned around and swam back across to rejoin the other athletes battling the ropes for a third attempt.

At that point, Ryan Atkins was already sipping a latte and reading the Miami Herald back in the festival area. The top 10 males had crossed the finish line long ago.  There was no check with my name on it and no trophy.  That orange wristband and an unshakeable sense of pride in accomplishment were all that was left to take home.  I wasn't about to let that go. 
On my third attempt, I painfully crawled along the top of the rope for about 50 ft before slipping under. That's when my will took over.  I WAS NOT GOING BACK!  Hand over hand, foot over foot, I muscled across and finally made it.  #nevergiveup  Sometimes timing and ranking just don't matter.  I will be wearing that wristband for at least a week. 👊 🐸 💪"

Comment: fullcolorstore said "Hello and welcome to Full Color Store. We do a lot of beautiful signs but also we teach you how to install its by yourself.
Follow the next steps and you will save money in installation.
1) Clean the surface with soap and water. Then use white vinegar to have an excellent adhesion to the surface.

2) We do not recommend to wrap plastic parts, they're porousy and contain wax particles that avoid the adhesive. But if you want to try it we recommend you to buy and use 3M primer (wrap vehicle) covering all the plastic surface. Let it dry for 5 minutes and continue.

3) Cover holes. If you decided to remove the car emblems, those leave (sometimes) holes on the surface. Use plain vinyl to cover the space, simulating (if possible) the shape to avoid to see the patch through the final wrap vinyl.

4) Cover the whole surface with your wrap vinyl and start to cover it. (We will teach you in another post How to do it). 5) Use heat to help you to mold the vinyl on deep zones.

6) Cut the vinyl around the handle, edges, etc. Remember to use a new or sharped blade to do this. 
That's it. You have a well wrapped piece of your vehicle (Partial wrap). If you have your own project, and need some #tips, do not hesitate to contact us. (Explicacion en Español disponible). We invite you to see our other post. If you have your own business or want to have one, do not hesitate to Follow us and Enjoy the information We share with You.  #Followme #creativity #marketingtool #marketing #business #signs #happy #goodprices #newimage #ideas #promotion #smallbusiness #retail #printing #installation #partialwrap #fullwrap #startingbusiness #letreros #negocios #publicidad #buenosprecios #tips"

Comment: jadi___ said "Was I hoping to place better so far? For sure. But who's fault is that? Mine. I'm capable of getting more reps in 15.1 and definitely capable of lifting heavier on 15.1a but I'm still happy with my placement, why? |

Since my birthday month in October I haven't really trained like I use to. Maybe two comp classes, an oly class and a class wod a week, at most. I was focusing more on having a life outside of CrossFit for a little while, which we all need from time to time.  I've also been on zero supplements. No protein shakes, fish oil, not even a multivitamin. Just food and not even really healthy food. Y'all know my struggle 🐷 lol. |

What does this tell me? That I've come a long way. That if I consistently give 110% again, eat right, take my supps and train insane I'm capable of so much more. |

I can make excuses that I work full time and have four children I need to care for but the truth is in the past I've trained 5-6 times a week and followed Invictus programming religiously and still made it happen. |

But with that said, I have to give credit to being #BooBooTrained by my coach @booboo_rayray31 @warriortraining_ with stepping back from training the way I have and mainly following his #warriortraining competition class I've still been able to keep up with some pretty amazing beasts. Thank you, Ray. I appreciate you |

What does this do to me? It makes me hungry. I'm ready to get on point again and start reaching my full potential that I haven't tapped into yet. Consistency is key and only I can make that happen and will. I'm on my second year of CrossFit, there's still so much more to explore and conquer. Can't wait 💪 |

4 more weeks to go #CrossFitOpen #CrossFitGamesOpen #TheOpenIsUponUs |
